app.use(function *(next){
    console.log(this.app.enableCache);
    //true
    this.app.enableCache = false;
 
    //just use this
    this.staticPath = &apos;static&apos;;
 
    yield *next;

//&#x5E94;&#x7528;&#x5171;&#x4EAB;&#x6570;&#x636E;&#xFF1A;ctx.state

// GET /shoes?order=desc&amp;shoe[color]=blue
req.query.order
// =&gt; &quot;desc&quot;
 
req.query.shoe.color
// =&gt; &quot;blue&quot;
 
// &#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x8DEF;&#x7531;&#x83B7;&#x53D6;Restful&#x98CE;&#x683C;&#x7684;URL&#x53C2;&#x6570;
app.get(&apos;/user/:id?&apos;, function userIdHandler(req, res) {
    console.log(req.params.id);
    res.send(&apos;GET&apos;);
})
 
//&#x83B7;&#x53D6;POST&#x6570;&#x636E;:&#x9700;&#x8981;body-parser&#x4E2D;&#x95F4;&#x4EF6;
var bodyParser = require(&apos;body-parser&apos;);

    console.log(req.body);

<span class="hljs-comment">// =&gt; &quot;desc&quot;</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// =&gt; &quot;blue&quot;</span>

// &#x83B7;&#x53D6;QueryString&#x53C2;&#x6570;
// GET /?action=delete&amp;id=1234
this.request.query
// =&gt; { action: &apos;delete&apos;, id: &apos;1234&apos; }
 
// &#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x8DEF;&#x7531;&#x83B7;&#x53D6;Restful&#x98CE;&#x683C;&#x7684;URL&#x53C2;&#x6570;
var route = require(&apos;koa-route&apos;);
app.use(route.get(&apos;/post/:id&apos;, function *(id){
    console.log(id);
    // =&gt; 1234
}));
 
// &#x83B7;&#x53D6;POST&#x6570;&#x636E;:&#x9700;&#x8981;co-body&#x4E2D;&#x95F4;&#x4EF6;
// Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded
// title=Test&amp;content=This+is+a+test+post
var parse = require(&apos;co-body&apos;);
app.use(route.post(&apos;/post/new&apos;, function *(){
    var post = yield parse(this.request);//this
    console.log(post);
    // =&gt; { title: &apos;Test&apos;, content: &apos;This is a test post&apos; }
}));" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="hljs javascript"><code>
<span class="hljs-comment">// &#x83B7;&#x53D6;QueryString&#x53C2;&#x6570;</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// GET /?action=delete&amp;id=1234</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.request.query
<span class="hljs-comment">// =&gt; { action: &apos;delete&apos;, id: &apos;1234&apos; }</span>
 
<span class="hljs-comment">// &#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x8DEF;&#x7531;&#x83B7;&#x53D6;Restful&#x98CE;&#x683C;&#x7684;URL&#x53C2;&#x6570;</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> route = <span class="hljs-built_in">require</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;koa-route&apos;</span>);

    <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(id);
    <span class="hljs-comment">// =&gt; 1234</span>
}));
 
<span class="hljs-comment">// &#x83B7;&#x53D6;POST&#x6570;&#x636E;:&#x9700;&#x8981;co-body&#x4E2D;&#x95F4;&#x4EF6;</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// title=Test&amp;content=This+is+a+test+post</span>

    setTimeout(resolve, ms);
  });
}

async function asyncPrint(value, ms) {
  await timeout(ms);
  console.log(value)
}

  <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(value)

    await somethingThatReturnsAPromise();
  } catch (err) {

  let docs = [{}, {}, {}];
  let promises = docs.map((doc) =&gt; db.post(doc));

  let results = await Promise.all(promises);
  console.log(results);
}

// &#x6216;&#x8005;&#x4F7F;&#x7528;&#x4E0B;&#x9762;&#x7684;&#x5199;&#x6CD5;

async function dbFuc(db) {
  let docs = [{}, {}, {}];
  let promises = docs.map((doc) =&gt; db.post(doc));

  let results = [];
  for (let promise of promises) {
    results.push(await promise);
  }
  console.log(results);

    name: &apos;Dot&apos;
}

    console.log(this.name)

dot()  // Dot

//bind &#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x4E0D;&#x4F1A;&#x7ACB;&#x5373;&#x6267;&#x884C;&#xFF0C;&#x800C;&#x662F;&#x8FD4;&#x56DE;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x6539;&#x53D8;&#x4E86;&#x4E0A;&#x4E0B;&#x6587; this &#x540E;&#x7684;&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x3002;
 //&#x800C;&#x539F;&#x51FD;&#x6570;printName &#x4E2D;&#x7684; this &#x5E76;&#x6CA1;&#x6709;&#x88AB;&#x6539;&#x53D8;&#xFF0C;&#x4F9D;&#x65E7;&#x6307;&#x5411;&#x5168;&#x5C40;&#x5BF9;&#x8C61; window&#x3002;" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="hljs javascript"><code><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> obj = {
    <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&apos;Dot&apos;</span>

function receiveMessage(event) {
  if (event.origin !== &apos;http://aaa.com&apos;) return;
  if (event.data === &apos;Hello World&apos;) {
      event.source.postMessage(&apos;Hello&apos;, event.origin);

    console.log(event.data);

function receiveMessage(<span class="hljs-keyword">event</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">event</span>.origin !== <span class="hljs-string">&apos;http://aaa.com&apos;</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (<span class="hljs-keyword">event</span>.data === <span class="hljs-string">&apos;Hello World&apos;</span>) {
      <span class="hljs-keyword">event</span>.<span class="hljs-keyword">source</span>.postMessage(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;Hello&apos;</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">event</span>.origin);
  } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
    console.<span class="hljs-keyword">log</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">event</span>.data);
  }

&lt;script&gt;
function checkHash(){
  var data = &apos;&apos;;
  //&#x6A21;&#x62DF;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x7B80;&#x5355;&#x7684;&#x53C2;&#x6570;&#x5904;&#x7406;&#x64CD;&#x4F5C;
  switch(location.hash){
    case &apos;#sayHello&apos;: data = &apos;HelloWorld&apos;;break;
    case &apos;#sayHi&apos;: data = &apos;HiWorld&apos;;break;
    default: break;
  }
  data &amp;&amp; callBack(&apos;#&apos;+data);
}
function callBack(hash){
  // ie&#x3001;chrome&#x7684;&#x5B89;&#x5168;&#x673A;&#x5236;&#x65E0;&#x6CD5;&#x4FEE;&#x6539;parent.location.hash&#xFF0C;&#x6240;&#x4EE5;&#x8981;&#x5229;&#x7528;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x4E2D;&#x95F4;&#x7684;www.a.com&#x57DF;&#x4E0B;&#x7684;&#x4EE3;&#x7406;iframe
  var proxy = document.createElement(&apos;iframe&apos;);
  proxy.style.display = &apos;none&apos;;
  proxy.src = &apos;http://localhost:8088/proxy.html&apos;+hash;  // &#x6CE8;&#x610F;&#x8BE5;&#x6587;&#x4EF6;&#x5728;&quot;www.a.com&quot;&#x57DF;&#x4E0B;
  document.body.appendChild(proxy);
}

<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">script</span>&gt;</span><span class="javascript">
<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">checkHash</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>)</span>{
  <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> data = <span class="hljs-string">&apos;&apos;</span>;
  <span class="hljs-comment">//&#x6A21;&#x62DF;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x7B80;&#x5355;&#x7684;&#x53C2;&#x6570;&#x5904;&#x7406;&#x64CD;&#x4F5C;</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span>(location.hash){
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-string">&apos;#sayHello&apos;</span>: data = <span class="hljs-string">&apos;HelloWorld&apos;</span>;<span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-string">&apos;#sayHi&apos;</span>: data = <span class="hljs-string">&apos;HiWorld&apos;</span>;<span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span>: <span class="hljs-keyword">break</span>;
  }
  data &amp;&amp; callBack(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;#&apos;</span>+data);
}
<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">callBack</span>(<span class="hljs-params">hash</span>)</span>{
  <span class="hljs-comment">// ie&#x3001;chrome&#x7684;&#x5B89;&#x5168;&#x673A;&#x5236;&#x65E0;&#x6CD5;&#x4FEE;&#x6539;parent.location.hash&#xFF0C;&#x6240;&#x4EE5;&#x8981;&#x5229;&#x7528;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x4E2D;&#x95F4;&#x7684;www.a.com&#x57DF;&#x4E0B;&#x7684;&#x4EE3;&#x7406;iframe</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> proxy = <span class="hljs-built_in">document</span>.createElement(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;iframe&apos;</span>);
  proxy.style.display = <span class="hljs-string">&apos;none&apos;</span>;
  proxy.src = <span class="hljs-string">&apos;http://localhost:8088/proxy.html&apos;</span>+hash;  <span class="hljs-comment">// &#x6CE8;&#x610F;&#x8BE5;&#x6587;&#x4EF6;&#x5728;&quot;www.a.com&quot;&#x57DF;&#x4E0B;</span>
  <span class="hljs-built_in">document</span>.body.appendChild(proxy);
}
<span class="hljs-built_in">window</span>.onload = checkHash;
</span><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">script</span>&gt;</span></code></pre><div class="widget-codetool" style="display:none"><div class="widget-codetool--inner"><span class="selectCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x5168;&#x9009;"></span> <span type="button" class="copyCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" data-clipboard-text="//&#x7531;&#x4E8E;&#x4E24;&#x4E2A;&#x9875;&#x9762;&#x4E0D;&#x5728;&#x540C;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x57DF;&#x4E0B;&#xFF0C;IE&#x3001;Chrome&#x4E0D;&#x5141;&#x8BB8;&#x4FEE;&#x6539;parent.location.hash&#x7684;&#x503C;&#xFF0C;&#x6240;&#x4EE5;&#x8981;&#x501F;&#x52A9;&#x4E8E;a.com&#x57DF;&#x540D;&#x4E0B;&#x7684;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x4EE3;&#x7406;iframe&#xFF0C;&#x8FD9;&#x91CC;&#x6709;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;a.com&#x4E0B;&#x7684;&#x4EE3;&#x7406;&#x6587;&#x4EF6;c.html&#x3002;Firefox&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x4FEE;&#x6539;&#x3002;
//c.html
&lt;script&gt;parent.parent.location.hash = self.location.hash.substring(1);  &lt;/script&gt;" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="hljs lasso"><code><span class="hljs-comment">//&#x7531;&#x4E8E;&#x4E24;&#x4E2A;&#x9875;&#x9762;&#x4E0D;&#x5728;&#x540C;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x57DF;&#x4E0B;&#xFF0C;IE&#x3001;Chrome&#x4E0D;&#x5141;&#x8BB8;&#x4FEE;&#x6539;parent.location.hash&#x7684;&#x503C;&#xFF0C;&#x6240;&#x4EE5;&#x8981;&#x501F;&#x52A9;&#x4E8E;a.com&#x57DF;&#x540D;&#x4E0B;&#x7684;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x4EE3;&#x7406;iframe&#xFF0C;&#x8FD9;&#x91CC;&#x6709;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;a.com&#x4E0B;&#x7684;&#x4EE3;&#x7406;&#x6587;&#x4EF6;c.html&#x3002;Firefox&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x4FEE;&#x6539;&#x3002;</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">//c.html</span>
&lt;script&gt;<span class="hljs-keyword">parent</span>.<span class="hljs-keyword">parent</span>.location.hash = <span class="hljs-built_in">self</span>.location.hash.substring(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>);  &lt;/script&gt;</code></pre><p>&#x76F4;&#x63A5;&#x8BBF;&#x95EE;a.html&#xFF0C;a.html&#x5411;b.html&#x53D1;&#x9001;&#x7684;&#x6D88;&#x606F;&#x4E3A;&#x201D;sayHi&#x201D;&#xFF1B;b.html&#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x6D88;&#x606F;&#x5224;&#x65AD;&#x8FD4;&#x56DE;&#x4E86;&#x201D;HiWorld&#x201D;&#xFF0C;&#x5E76;&#x901A;&#x8FC7;c.html&#x6539;&#x53D8;&#x4E86;location.hash&#x7684;&#x503C;</p><p><span class="img-wrap"><img data-src="/img/bVbhuZu?w=1294&amp;h=90" src="https://static.alili.tech/img/bVbhuZu?w=1294&amp;h=90" alt="clipboard.png" title="clipboard.png" style="cursor:pointer"></span></p><p><strong>AJAX</strong><br>&#x540C;&#x6E90;&#x653F;&#x7B56;&#x89C4;&#x5B9A;&#xFF0C;AJAX&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#x53EA;&#x80FD;&#x53D1;&#x7ED9;&#x540C;&#x6E90;&#x7684;&#x7F51;&#x5740;&#xFF0C;&#x5426;&#x5219;&#x5C31;&#x62A5;&#x9519;&#x3002;</p><p>&#x9664;&#x4E86;&#x67B6;&#x8BBE;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#x5668;&#x4EE3;&#x7406;&#xFF08;&#x6D4F;&#x89C8;&#x5668;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#x540C;&#x6E90;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#x5668;&#xFF0C;&#x518D;&#x7531;&#x540E;&#x8005;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#x5916;&#x90E8;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#xFF09;&#xFF0C;&#x6709;&#x4E09;&#x79CD;&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x89C4;&#x907F;&#x8FD9;&#x4E2A;&#x9650;&#x5236;&#x3002;</p><ol><li>JSONP</li><li>WebSocket</li><li>CORS</li></ol><p><strong>JSONP</strong><br>JSONP&#x662F;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#x5668;&#x4E0E;&#x5BA2;&#x6237;&#x7AEF;&#x8DE8;&#x6E90;&#x901A;&#x4FE1;&#x7684;&#x5E38;&#x7528;&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x3002;&#x6700;&#x5927;&#x7279;&#x70B9;&#x5C31;&#x662F;&#x7B80;&#x5355;&#x9002;&#x7528;&#xFF0C;&#x8001;&#x5F0F;&#x6D4F;&#x89C8;&#x5668;&#x5168;&#x90E8;&#x652F;&#x6301;&#xFF0C;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#x5668;&#x6539;&#x9020;&#x975E;&#x5E38;&#x5C0F;&#x3002;</p><p>&#x5B83;&#x7684;&#x57FA;&#x672C;&#x601D;&#x60F3;&#x662F;&#xFF0C;&#x7F51;&#x9875;&#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x6DFB;&#x52A0;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&lt;script&gt;&#x5143;&#x7D20;&#xFF0C;&#x5411;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#x5668;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;JSON&#x6570;&#x636E;&#xFF0C;&#x8FD9;&#x79CD;&#x505A;&#x6CD5;&#x4E0D;&#x53D7;&#x540C;&#x6E90;&#x653F;&#x7B56;&#x9650;&#x5236;&#xFF1B;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#x5668;&#x6536;&#x5230;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#x540E;&#xFF0C;&#x5C06;&#x6570;&#x636E;&#x653E;&#x5728;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x6307;&#x5B9A;&#x540D;&#x5B57;&#x7684;&#x56DE;&#x8C03;&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x91CC;&#x4F20;&#x56DE;&#x6765;&#x3002;</p><p>&#x9996;&#x5148;&#xFF0C;&#x7F51;&#x9875;&#x52A8;&#x6001;&#x63D2;&#x5165;&lt;script&gt;&#x5143;&#x7D20;&#xFF0C;&#x7531;&#x5B83;&#x5411;&#x8DE8;&#x6E90;&#x7F51;&#x5740;&#x53D1;&#x51FA;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#x3002;</p><div class="widget-codetool" style="display:none"><div class="widget-codetool--inner"><span class="selectCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x5168;&#x9009;"></span> <span type="button" class="copyCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" data-clipboard-text="function addScriptTag(src) {
  var script = document.createElement(&apos;script&apos;);
  script.setAttribute(&quot;type&quot;,&quot;text/javascript&quot;);
  script.src = src;
  document.body.appendChild(script);
}

window.onload = function () {
  addScriptTag(&apos;http://example.com/ip?callback=foo&apos;);
}

function foo(data) {
  console.log(&apos;Your public IP address is: &apos; + data.ip);
};
//&#x4E0A;&#x9762;&#x4EE3;&#x7801;&#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x52A8;&#x6001;&#x6DFB;&#x52A0;&lt;script&gt;&#x5143;&#x7D20;&#xFF0C;&#x5411;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#x5668;example.com&#x53D1;&#x51FA;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#x3002;

  <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> script = <span class="hljs-built_in">document</span>.createElement(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;script&apos;</span>);

<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">foo</span>(<span class="hljs-params">data</span>) </span>{

<span class="hljs-comment">//&#x4E0A;&#x9762;&#x4EE3;&#x7801;&#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x52A8;&#x6001;&#x6DFB;&#x52A0;&lt;script&gt;&#x5143;&#x7D20;&#xFF0C;&#x5411;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#x5668;example.com&#x53D1;&#x51FA;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#x3002;</span>

CORS</h2><p>&#x5B83;&#x5141;&#x8BB8;&#x6D4F;&#x89C8;&#x5668;&#x5411;&#x8DE8;&#x6E90;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#x5668;&#xFF0C;&#x53D1;&#x51FA;XMLHttpRequest&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#xFF0C;&#x4ECE;&#x800C;&#x514B;&#x670D;&#x4E86;AJAX&#x53EA;&#x80FD;&#x540C;&#x6E90;&#x4F7F;&#x7528;&#x7684;&#x9650;&#x5236;&#x3002;</p><p><strong>&#x4E24;&#x79CD;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;</strong></p><p>&#x6D4F;&#x89C8;&#x5668;&#x5C06;CORS&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#x5206;&#x6210;&#x4E24;&#x7C7B;&#xFF1A;&#x7B80;&#x5355;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#xFF08;simple &#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x662F;&#x4EE5;&#x4E0B;&#x4E09;&#x79CD;&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x4E4B;&#x4E00;&#xFF1A;</p><ul><li>HEAD</li><li>GET</li><li>POST</li></ul><p>&#xFF08;2&#xFF09;HTTP&#x7684;&#x5934;&#x4FE1;&#x606F;&#x4E0D;&#x8D85;&#x51FA;&#x4EE5;&#x4E0B;&#x51E0;&#x79CD;&#x5B57;&#x6BB5;&#xFF1A;</p><ul><li>Accept</li><li>Accept-Language</li><li>Content-Language</li><li>Last-Event-ID</li><li>Content-Type&#xFF1A;&#x53EA;&#x9650;&#x4E8E;&#x4E09;&#x4E2A;&#x503C;application/x-www-form-urlencoded&#x3001;<br>multipart/form-data&#x3001;text/plain</li></ul><p>&#x51E1;&#x662F;&#x4E0D;&#x540C;&#x65F6;&#x6EE1;&#x8DB3;&#x4E0A;&#x9762;&#x4E24;&#x4E2A;&#x6761;&#x4EF6;&#xFF0C;&#x5C31;&#x5C5E;&#x4E8E;&#x975E;&#x7B80;&#x5355;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#x3002;</p><p><strong>&#x7B80;&#x5355;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;</strong></p><p>&#x5BF9;&#x4E8E;&#x7B80;&#x5355;&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#xFF0C;&#x6D4F;&#x89C8;&#x5668;&#x76F4;&#x63A5;&#x53D1;&#x51FA;CORS&#x8BF7;&#x6C42;&#x3002;&#x5177;&#x4F53;&#x6765;&#x8BF4;&#xFF0C;&#x5C31;&#x662F;&#x5728;&#x5934;&#x4FE1;&#x606F;&#x4E4B;&#x4E2D;&#xFF0C;&#x589E;&#x52A0;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;Origin&#x5B57;&#x6BB5;&#x3002;</p><div </span></code></pre><p>&#x5982;&#x679C;Origin&#x6307;&#x5B9A;&#x7684;&#x6E90;&#xFF0C;&#x4E0D;&#x5728;&#x8BB8;&#x53EF;&#x8303;&#x56F4;&#x5185;&#xFF0C;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#x5668;&#x4F1A;&#x8FD4;&#x56DE;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x6B63;&#x5E38;&#x7684;HTTP&#x56DE;&#x5E94;&#x3002;&#x6D4F;&#x89C8;&#x5668;&#x53D1;&#x73B0;&#xFF0C;&#x8FD9;&#x4E2A;&#x56DE;&#x5E94;&#x7684;&#x5934;&#x4FE1;&#x606F;&#x6CA1;&#x6709;&#x5305;&#x542B;Access-Control-Allow-Origin&#x5B57;&#x6BB5;&#xFF08;&#x8BE6;&#x89C1;&#x4E0B;&#x6587;&#xFF09;&#xFF0C;&#x5C31;&#x77E5;&#x9053;&#x51FA;&#x9519;&#x4E86;&#xFF0C;&#x4ECE;&#x800C;&#x629B;&#x51FA;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x9519;&#x8BEF;&#xFF0C;&#x88AB;XMLHttpRequest&#x7684;onerror&#x56DE;&#x8C03;&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x6355;&#x83B7;&#x3002;&#x6CE8;&#x610F;&#xFF0C;&#x8FD9;&#x79CD;&#x9519;&#x8BEF;&#x65E0;&#x6CD5;&#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x72B6;&#x6001;&#x7801;&#x8BC6;&#x522B;&#xFF0C;&#x56E0;&#x4E3A;HTTP&#x56DE;&#x5E94;&#x7684;&#x72B6;&#x6001;&#x7801;&#x6709;&#x53EF;&#x80FD;&#x662F;200&#x3002;</p><p>&#x5982;&#x679C;Origin&#x6307;&#x5B9A;&#x7684;&#x57DF;&#x540D;&#x5728;&#x8BB8;&#x53EF;&#x8303;&#x56F4;&#x5185;&#xFF0C;&#x670D;&#x52A1;&#x5668;&#x8FD4;&#x56DE;&#x7684;&#x54CD;&#x5E94;&#xFF0C;&#x4F1A;&#x591A;&#x51FA;&#x51E0;&#x4E2A;&#x5934;&#x4FE1;&#x606F;&#x5B57;&#x6BB5;&#x3002;</p><div class="widget-codetool" style="display:none"><div class="widget-codetool--inner"><span class="selectCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x5168;&#x9009;"></span> <span type="button" class="copyCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" data-clipboard-text="Access-Control-Allow-Origin: http://api.bob.com

var EventUtil = {
   addHandlers: function (element, type, handlers) {
      if (element.addEventListener) {
         element.addEventListener(type, handlers, false);
      } else if (element.attachEvent) {
         element.attachEvent(on + type, handlers);
      } else {
         element[&apos;on&apos; + type] = handlers;
      }
   },
   removeHandlers: function (element, type, handlers) {
      if (element.removeEventListener) {
         element.removeEventListener(type, handlers, false);
      } else if (element.detachEvent) {
         element.detachEvent(on + type, handlers);
      } else {
         element[&apos;on&apos; + type] = null;
      }
   }
};" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="hljs scala"><code><span class="hljs-comment">//&#x521B;&#x5EFA;&#x7684;&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x662F;addHandlers(),removeHandlers(),&#x8FD9;&#x4E24;&#x4E2A;&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x5C5E;&#x4E8E;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x53EB;EventUtil&#x7684;&#x5BF9;&#x8C61;;&#x4F46;&#x662F;&#x8FD9;&#x4E2A;&#x6CA1;&#x6709;&#x8003;&#x8651;&#x5230;IE&#x4E2D;&#x4F5C;&#x7528;&#x57DF;&#x7684;&#x95EE;&#x9898;&#xFF0C;&#x4E0D;&#x8FC7;&#x5C31;&#x6DFB;&#x52A0;&#x548C;&#x79FB;&#x9664;&#x4E8B;&#x4EF6;&#x8FD8;&#x662F;&#x8DB3;&#x591F;&#x7684;&#x3002;</span>

}" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="hljs actionscript"><code><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">concatArr</span><span class="hljs-params">(arr1, arr2)</span></span>{
  <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> arr = arr1.concat(arr2);
  arr = unique1(arr);<span class="hljs-comment">//&#x518D;&#x5F15;&#x7528;&#x4E0A;&#x9762;&#x7684;&#x4EFB;&#x610F;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x53BB;&#x91CD;&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> arr;
}</code></pre><p><strong>&#x4E8C;&#x3001;Array.prototype.push.apply()</strong></p><p>&#x601D;&#x8DEF;&#xFF1A;&#x8BE5;&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x4F18;&#x70B9;&#x662F;&#x4E0D;&#x4F1A;&#x4EA7;&#x751F;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x65B0;&#x7684;&#x6570;&#x7EC4;</p><div class="widget-codetool" style="display:none"><div class="widget-codetool--inner"><span class="selectCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x5168;&#x9009;"></span> <span type="button" class="copyCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" data-clipboard-text="var a = [1, 2, 3];
var b = [4, 5, 6];
Array.prototype.push.apply(a, b);//a=[1,2,3,4,5,6]
//&#x7B49;&#x6548;&#x4E8E;:a.push.apply(a, b);
//&#x4E5F;&#x7B49;&#x6548;&#x4E8E;[].push.apply(a, b); 
function concatArray(arr1,arr2){
  Array.prototype.push.apply(arr1, arr2);
  arr1 = unique1(arr1);
  return arr1;
}
" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="hljs javascript"><code><span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> a = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>];

    name: &apos;chris&apos;,
    sex: &apos;male&apos;,
    age: 26,
    son: {
        sonname: &apos;&#x5927;&#x718A;&apos;,
        sonsex: &apos;male&apos;,
        sonage: 1
    }
};

    console.log(name + &apos; &apos; + sex + &apos; &apos; + age);
}

//&#x53D8;&#x91CF;&#x540D;&#x4E0E;&#x5BF9;&#x8C61;&#x5C5E;&#x6027;&#x540D;&#x4E0D;&#x4E00;&#x81F4;&#x89E3;&#x6784;&#xFF1A;

    sex: &apos;male&apos;,
    age: 26
};

//&#x5D4C;&#x5957;&#x5BF9;&#x8C61;&#x89E3;&#x6784;&#xFF1A;

var bar = function(...args) {
    for (let el of args) {
        console.log(el);
    }
}

bar(1, 2, 3, 4);
//1
//2
//3
//4

bar = function(a, ...args) {
    console.log(a);
    console.log(args);
}

bar(1, 2, 3, 4);
//1
//[ 2, 3, 4 ]" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="hljs actionscript"><code><span class="hljs-comment">//&#x4E3B;&#x8981;&#x7528;&#x4E8E;&#x4E0D;&#x5B9A;&#x53C2;&#x6570;&#xFF0C;&#x6240;&#x4EE5;ES6&#x5F00;&#x59CB;&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x4E0D;&#x518D;&#x4F7F;&#x7528;arguments&#x5BF9;&#x8C61;</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> bar = <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span><span class="hljs-params">(<span class="hljs-rest_arg">...args</span>)</span> </span>{
    <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (let el of args) {
        console.log(el);
    }

<span class="hljs-comment">//1</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">//2</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">//3</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">//4</span>

    console.log(a);
    console.log(args);
}

<span class="hljs-comment">//1</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">//[ 2, 3, 4 ]</span></code></pre><p><strong>rest&#x8FD0;&#x7B97;&#x7B26;&#x914D;&#x5408;&#x89E3;&#x6784;&#x4F7F;&#x7528;&#xFF1A;</strong></p><div class="widget-codetool" style="display:none"><div class="widget-codetool--inner"><span class="selectCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x5168;&#x9009;"></span> <span type="button" class="copyCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" data-clipboard-text="var [a, ...rest] = [1, 2, 3, 4];

  base : 1,
    
  add : function(a) {
    var f = v =&gt; v + this.base;
    return f(a);
  },

  addThruCall: function(a) {
    var f = v =&gt; v + this.base;
    var b = {
      base : 2
    };
            
    return f.call(b, a);
  }
};

console.log(adder.add(1));         // &#x8F93;&#x51FA; 2

function A(){
      var i=0;
      return function b(){
              return (++i);
      };
};

var v=A();
v();    //1
v();    //2


//&#x7BAD;&#x5934;&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x4F53;&#x7684;&#x95ED;&#x5305;&#xFF08; i=0 &#x662F;&#x9ED8;&#x8BA4;&#x53C2;&#x6570;&#xFF09;
var Add = (i=0) =&gt; {return (() =&gt; (++i) )};
var v = Add();
v();           //1
v();           //2

//&#x56E0;&#x4E3A;&#x4EC5;&#x6709;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x8FD4;&#x56DE;&#xFF0C;return &#x53CA;&#x62EC;&#x53F7;&#xFF08;&#xFF09;&#x4E5F;&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x7701;&#x7565;

<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">A</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>)</span>{
      <span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> i=<span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
      <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">b</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>)</span>{
              <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (++i);
      };
};

<span class="hljs-keyword">var</span> v=A();
v();    <span class="hljs-comment">//1</span>
v();    <span class="hljs-comment">//2</span>
